# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
m = row (length)
n = columns (length)
c = count of paths
dfs (m, n, xorsum):

if (m == M && n == N):
    if(xorsum == k):
        c++
    return 

xorsum ^= nums[m][n] // for this iteration m = last column

// m++ (increment rows with same column) => going down

// check for boundary
if (m+1 < M): // check for row boundary
    dfs(n, m+1, xorsum)

//n++
    if ( n+1 < N): // checking for column boundary
    dfs (m, n+1, xorsum)



 ^WabuSyr1

%%
